000440_9269cfd8-259d-e978-3df8-f6a8ff485447STANDOC_48
(generic warning) Hanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="_9269cfd8-259d-e978-3df8-f6a8ff485447" obligation="normative">
<title id="_788ce232-71b7-6ad3-d498-16982436c341">Introduction</title>
<p id="_22239734-ff21-c8c4-3a97-dae5ea2408c1">The W3C Semantic Web Activity defines a collection of technologies that enables a web of data where information is easily shared and reused across applications. Some key pieces of this technology stack are the Resource Description Framework (RDF) data model <xref target="RDF" style="short"/>, <xref target="RDFS" style="short"/>, the OWL Web Ontology Language <xref target="OWL2" style="short"/> and the SPARQL Protocol and RDF Query Language <xref target="sparql_protocol" style="short"/>.</p>

<clause id="_24045273-fc87-eb7a-1ac9-02e8da031a4e" obligation="normative">
2



000594_cc517748-6d39-121e-d4cd-efa9e3e4fcb0STANDOC_48
(generic warning) Hanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="_cc517748-6d39-121e-d4cd-efa9e3e4fcb0" obligation="normative">
<title id="_c8c660e3-f8d3-3b8b-b9b8-1eb6a7a7183d">Core</title>
<p id="_814b8408-edc1-1290-1d41-09c907c9adfa" anchor="core">This clause establishes the <strong>Core</strong> Requirements class, with IRI <tt>/req/core</tt>, which has a corresponding Conformance Class, <strong>Core</strong>, with IRI <tt>/conf/core</tt>. These Requirements define a set of classes and properties for representing geospatial data. The resulting vocabularyan ontologycan be used to construct SPARQL graph patterns for querying appropriately modeled geospatial data. The RDFS and OWL vocabularies have both been used so that the vocabulary can be understood by systems that support only RDFS entailment and by systems that support OWL-based reasoning.</p>

<p id="_5cb1cf08-f376-d09c-3d9d-74e2730512d8">The figure below gives an overview of the classes and properties defined by GeoSPARQL in the <strong>Core</strong>, <strong>Topology Vocabulary Extension</strong> and <strong>Geometry Extension</strong>, <strong>Geometry Topology Extension</strong> and <strong>RDFS Entailment Extension</strong> Conformance Classes.</p>
2



000612_884eb2b0-dadd-29b6-0733-c6475ac84c48STANDOC_48
(generic warning) Hanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="_884eb2b0-dadd-29b6-0733-c6475ac84c48" obligation="normative">
<title id="_3c14916f-7955-e163-6c60-9624005e3c85">Classes</title>
<p id="_7e92cf5b-67e5-9d20-b957-bc881f4c774d">Two main classes are defined: <eref bibitemid="Class_ geo" citeas=""> <localityStack> <locality type="anchor"> <referenceFrom>SpatialObject</referenceFrom> </locality> </localityStack> <display-text>geo:SpatialObject</display-text> </eref> and <eref bibitemid="Class_ geo" citeas=""> <localityStack> <locality type="anchor"> <referenceFrom>Feature</referenceFrom> </locality> </localityStack> <display-text>Feature</display-text> </eref>.</p>

<p id="_f11fcdd0-c1aa-92cd-75c0-e77e8e99555d">Two container classes are defined: <eref bibitemid="Class_ geo" citeas=""> <localityStack> <locality type="anchor"> <referenceFrom>SpatialObjectCollection</referenceFrom> </locality> </localityStack> <display-text>Spatial Object Collection</display-text> </eref> and <eref bibitemid="Class_ geo" citeas=""> <localityStack> <locality type="anchor"> <referenceFrom>FeatureCollection</referenceFrom> </locality> </localityStack> <display-text>Feature Collection</display-text> </eref>.</p>
2

001038_ae7f6818-b918-90c0-aa18-8493db54c451STANDOC_48
(generic warning) Hanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="_ae7f6818-b918-90c0-aa18-8493db54c451" obligation="normative">
<title id="_8f07b2bc-9955-f983-758f-67e23c509fcb">Topology Vocabulary Extension</title>
<p id="_7a4e12fc-f391-5db4-91f0-1bfaba6115ab">This clause establishes the <em>Topology Vocabulary Extension</em> parameterized Requirements class. The IRI base is <tt>/req/topology-vocab-extension</tt>, which has a single corresponding Conformance Class <em>Topology Vocabulary Extension</em>, with IRI <tt>/conf/topology-vocab-extension</tt>. This Requirements class defines a vocabulary for asserting and querying topological relations between spatial objects. The class is parameterized so that different families of topological relations may be used, such as RCC8 and Egenhofer. These relations are generalized so that they may connect features as well as geometries.</p>

<requirement id="_20e2b009-2e89-b552-bd0c-83679cf4fb92" model="ogc" type="class" anchor="/req/topology-vocab-extension">
2



001291_407b6738-c387-c083-57c4-272e0dfc7660STANDOC_48
(generic warning) Hanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="_407b6738-c387-c083-57c4-272e0dfc7660" obligation="normative">
<title id="_50027848-3d87-bf80-e859-d1cf7ff2c12b">Geometry Extension</title>
<p id="_212588d0-c830-e0b1-cb4c-54b96242446a">This clause defines the <em>Geometry Extension</em> parameterized Requirements class with the base IRI <tt>/req/geometry-extension</tt>. There is a single corresponding conformance class <em>Geometry Extension</em>, with the IRI <tt>/conf/geometry-extension</tt>. These Requirements define a vocabulary for asserting and querying information about geometry data, and define query functions for operating on geometry data.</p>

<requirement id="_58a94f35-6649-5bb3-228a-f379011dce92" model="ogc" type="class" anchor="/req/geometry-extension">
2



001464_f010a600-fd74-e8f2-de43-2961a25e7233STANDOC_48
(generic warning) Hanging paragraph in clause

<title id="_34043534-5962-4757-78e1-e5e9bc352503">Geometry Class</title>
<p id="_aed86530-fc9b-8229-c8c1-4a385cd1c05f">A single root geometry class is defined: <eref bibitemid="Class_ geo" citeas=""> <localityStack> <locality type="anchor"> <referenceFrom>Geometry</referenceFrom> </locality> </localityStack> <display-text>geo:Geometry</display-text> </eref>. In addition, properties are defined for describing geometry data and for associating geometries with features.</p>

<p id="_19b018fb-41fe-6292-1edd-0696a154513b">One container class is defined: <eref bibitemid="Class_ geo" citeas=""> <localityStack> <locality type="anchor"> <referenceFrom>GeometryCollection</referenceFrom> </locality> </localityStack> <display-text>Geometry Collection</display-text> </eref>.</p>

<p id="_f5fdbf72-c3b4-dab4-19c5-7ae8685a895b">Properties are defined for describing geometry metadata.</p>

001748_1fe0ec12-2c83-8f09-f0ee-173c3e11a228STANDOC_48
(generic warning) Hanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="_1fe0ec12-2c83-8f09-f0ee-173c3e11a228" obligation="normative">
<title id="_e3225d1d-338e-9318-64ac-49b4c911f7e0">Geometry Serializations</title>
<p id="_ad1888bc-7e6f-99c6-6fec-5853383fd1a9">This section establishes the Requirements class for representing Geometry data in RDF literals, according to different non-RDF systems.</p>

<p id="_a770367d-74cd-7c7b-7749-40dcb2a499fa">GeoSPARQL presents specializations of the <tt>geo:hasSerialization</tt> property for indicating particular serializations and specialized datatype literals for containing them. It does not provide comprehensive definitions of their content since these are given in standards external to GeoSPARQL, all of which are referenced.</p>

<p id="_0b16516e-8cca-e3e8-68e6-5f1294cd9179">This section establishes the requirements for representing Geometry data in RDF based on Extended Well-Known Binary (EWKB) as defined by <em>Simple Features Access</em> <xref target="OGC06-103r4" style="short"/> <xref target="ISO19125-1" style="short"/>. 003107geometry_topology_extensionSTANDOC_48
(generic warning) Hanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="_c187f7a7-57a9-5c9d-d8f8-a0682047b3b4" anchor="geometry_topology_extension" obligation="normative">
<title id="_c79c76b0-7f0b-241a-43f8-6f3e04c299bd">Geometry Topology Extension</title>
<p id="_1a97fe5c-3865-508d-e1ed-a71520f06e50">This clause establishes the <em>Geometry Topology Extension</em> parameterized Requirements class with base IRI <tt>/req/geometry-topology-extension</tt>, which defines a collection of topological query functions that operate on geometry literals. These Requirements are parameterized to give implementations flexibility in the topological relation families and geometry serializations that they choose to support. These Requirements have a single corresponding conformance class <em>Geometry Topology Extension</em>, with IRI <tt>/conf/geometry-topology-extension</tt>.</p>

<p id="_29bde281-15b1-f35a-bb94-5661d8977033">The Dimensionally Extended Nine Intersection Model (DE-9IM) <xref target="DE-9IM" style="short"/> has been used to define the relation tested by the query functions introduced in this section. Each query function is associated with a defining DE-9IM intersection pattern. Possible pattern values are:</p>

<title id="_4adc8917-daea-51ea-0604-32e7c2d7b697">RDFS Entailment Extension</title>
<p id="_71963777-2dd1-2b50-aada-4f2a23f0064c">This clause establishes the <em>RDFS Entailment Extension</em> parameterized Requirements class with base IRI <tt>/req/rdfs-entailment-extension</tt>, which defines a mechanism for matching implicitly-derived RDF triples in GeoSPARQL queries. This class is parameterized to give implementations flexibility in the topological relation families and geometry types that they choose to support. These Requirements have a single corresponding conformance class <em>RDFS Entailment Extension</em>, <tt>with IRI /conf/rdfs-entailment-extension</tt>.</p>

003378_b792bad0-11b0-f5b6-9620-83150890f1cfSTANDOC_48
(generic warning) Hanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="_b792bad0-11b0-f5b6-9620-83150890f1cf" obligation="normative">
<title id="_18dc5c38-9101-a9ed-6cd4-e88967dd25ec">Query Rewrite Extension</title>
<p id="_09cfd1e6-7437-9289-2958-8d4249cd9cb7">This clause establishes the <em>Query Rewrite Extension</em> parameterized Requirements class with base IRI <tt>/req/query-rewrite-extension</tt>, which has a single corresponding conformance class <em>Query Rewrite Extension</em>, with IRI <tt>/conf/query-rewrite-extension</tt>. These Requirements define a set of RIF rules <xref target="RIF" style="short"/> that use topological extension functions defined in <xref target="geometry_extension" style="short"/> to establish the existence of direct topological predicates defined in <xref target="vocabulary_extension" style="short"/>. One possible implementation strategy is to transform a given query by expanding a triple pattern involving a direct spatial predicate into a series of triple patterns and an invocation of the corresponding extension function as specified in the RIF rule.</p>

<requirement id="_eda33512-ecf1-5d94-bf89-3d59cfab6a52" model="ogc" type="class" anchor="/req/query-rewrite-extension">

003612_2291c2f9-cfad-5998-ad7d-671e6ef02b55STANDOC_48
(generic warning) Hanging paragraph in clause
<annex id="_2291c2f9-cfad-5998-ad7d-671e6ef02b55" obligation="normative">
<title id="_470614e0-369e-cd47-ac8c-e0c157b1a785">Abstract Test Suite</title>
<floating-title id="_6c4825b5-5b33-43be-8438-e76319911fee" depth="2" type="floating-title">A.0. Overview</floating-title>
<p id="_5a7783ec-360f-3488-bdc8-06a9073c4046">This Annex lists tests for the Conformance Classes defined in the main body sections of this Specification with links to their Requirements and test purpose method and type. Conformance classes may be used to signify the compatibility of a given implementation to parts of the GeoSPARQL standard. They may be stated as part of a SPARQL 1.1 Service Description  <xref target="SPARQLSERVDESC" style="short"/> .</p>

<title id="_e810a36f-6a97-d764-646a-078f233784bf">CQL / GeoSPARQL Mapping</title>
<floating-title id="_f50fc34a-1e4d-98ab-f86c-fff66d531dea" depth="2" type="floating-title">F.0. Overview</floating-title>
<p id="_2e54137d-3c61-c070-da31-72ee03391821">This annex presents a mapping between the Common Query Language(CQL) <xref target="CQLDEF" style="short"/> and GeoSPARQL as well as generic SPARQL <xref target="sparql_protocol" style="short"/>. This is likely of relevance to the delivery of GeoSPARQL data via systems such as the OGCs Web Feature Service <xref target="WFS" style="short"/> and OGC API Features <xref target="OGCAPIF" style="short"/> which implement CQL.</p>
